country_event = {
    id = 836592378
    title = "The Fate of Malaysia"
    desc = "MALAYSIAFATE"
    picture = "malaysia_fate"
    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = "We simply aim to unify the administration of the Malay peninsula."
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = JOH
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = PHG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = PRK
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = SLG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = JOH }
				any_owned_province = { is_core = JOH }
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			any_owned = {
				limit = { is_core = JOH }
				secede_province = THIS
			}
		}
		JOH = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = JOH
			}
		}
		SLG = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = SLG
			}
		}
		PHG = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = PHG
			}
		}
		PRK = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = PRK
			}
		}
		ENG_1384 = { add_core = MLY }
		ENG_1391 = { add_core = MLY }
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_core = MLY
				is_core = THIS
			}
			remove_core = MLY
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = malay }
			militancy = -6
		}
		1388 = { remove_core = MLY }
		1386 = { remove_core = MLY }

		1388 = { add_core = MLY }
		1386 = { add_core = MLY }
		1384 = { add_core = MLY }

    }

    option = {
        name = "The new Malaysian state shall have the goal of uniting the region!"

			limit = {
				tag = JOH
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS

			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}

			limit = {
				tag = PHG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}

			limit = {
				tag = PRK

					in_sphere = THIS

			}

		}
    }

    }

				}
			}

    }
}

    id = 191339
    title = "The Battle of Socabaya"
    desc = "SOCABAYA"
    fire_only_once = yes
    picture = "totally_not_ingavi"
    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
    trigger = {
		year = 1836
		tag = BOL
		SPU = { owns = 2304 }
		war_with = PEU
		month = 2
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = bolivia_annexes_peru
			NOT = { has_global_flag = eighteenthirty_startdate }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { 2304 = { country_units_in_province = PEU } } 
				SPU = { controls = 2304 }
			}
			PEU = { ai = yes }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = { NOT = { year = 1837 } OR = { ai = no PEU = { ai = no } } }
			AND = { NOT = { year = 1838 } ai = yes PEU = { ai = yes } }
		}
    }
    option = {
        name = "Huzzah!"
		end_war = PEU
		country_event = 16051934
		CLN = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = gov_legit_in_question duration = 60 }
		}
		create_vassal = PEU
    }
}

			}
		}
